<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пригодный.html>приго́дный</a> (10789)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годный.html>го́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пригодный.html>приго́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prigódnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>suitable (for), fit (for), good (for) (appropriate to a certain occasion)</li>
<li>applicable, eligible</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">го́жий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">góžij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*goditi</i>. </p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">folklore or poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> beautiful, good-looking</li>

***пригородный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пригородный.html>при́городный</a> (11004)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пригород.html>при́город</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prígorod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пригородный.html>при́городный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prígorodnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>suburban</li>
<li>local
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пригородный.html>при́городное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prígorodnoje</b> dvižénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">local traffic/service</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пригородный.html>при́городный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prígorodnyj</b> pójezd</i> ― <span class="e-translation">commuter train</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пригород.html>при́город</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prígorod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">górod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:городок.html>городо́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gorodók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:готовить.html>гото́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gotóvitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приготовить.html>пригото́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prigotóvitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:готовить.html>гото́вить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приготовлять.html>приготовля́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пригота́вливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to prepare, to make ready</li>
<li>to cook</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приготовить.html>пригото́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prigotóvitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приготовиться.html>пригото́виться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prigotóvitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:готовиться.html>гото́виться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приготовляться.html>приготовля́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пригота́вливаться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get ready, to prepare oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приготовиться.html>пригото́вились</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мену</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní <b>prigotóvilisʹ</b> k ekzámenu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they are ready for the exam</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приготовить.html>пригото́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prigotóvitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***приграничный.html

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пригреть.html>пригре́вший</a> (19743)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***придавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:придавать.html>придава́ть</a> (3607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придать.html>прида́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pridátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придавать.html>придава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pridavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придать.html>прида́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give, to impart; to attach</li>
<li>to increase, to strengthen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:придавать.html>придава́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:смелость.html>сме́лости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pridavátʹ</b> smélosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to increase braveness</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***придавить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:придавить.html>придави́ть</a> (7974)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придавить.html>придави́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pridavítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придавливать.html>прида́вливать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to press <i>(against)</i>, to press down <i>(against)</i>, to weigh down <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:придавить.html>придави́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>ка́мнем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pridavítʹ</b> kámnem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to press down under/with a stone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***придавливать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:придавливать.html>прида́вливать</a> (31613)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придавить.html>придави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pridavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придавливать.html>прида́вливать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pridávlivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придавить.html>придави́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to press <i>(against)</i>, to press down <i>(against)</i>, to weigh down <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:придавливать.html>прида́вливать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>ка́мнем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pridávlivatʹ</b> kámnem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to press down under/with a stone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ние</a> (23526)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pridánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>giving, conferring, imparting, communication
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ния</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dlja <b>pridánija</b> síly</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">(in order) to give strength</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ния</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:законный.html>зако́нной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dlja <b>pridánija</b> zakónnoj síly</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">(in order) to validate; (in order) to make legally binding</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
